    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer15362598734958598836">One kiss lasts a moment. But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. One boy. One girl. A bond that is forged in an instant and cherished for a decade.   <span id="freeText15362598734958598836" style="display:none">One kiss lasts a moment. But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. One boy. One girl. A bond that is forged in an instant and cherished for a decade. A bond that neither time nor distance can break. A bond that will last forever. Or so they believe. <br /><br />When seventeen-year-old Rune Kristiansen returns from his native Norway to the sleepy town of Blossom Grove, Georgia, where he befriended Poppy Litchfield as a child, he has just one thing on his mind. Why did the girl who was one half of his soul, who promised to wait faithfully for his return, cut him off without a word of explanation? Rune's heart was broken two years ago when Poppy fell silent. When he discovers the truth, he finds that the greatest heartache is yet to come. <br /><br />A stand-alone young adult tearjerker romance, recommended for ages fourteen and up.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=young-adult-new-adult">young-adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=pissed-me-the-fuck-off">pissed-me-the-fuck-off</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=1-stars">1-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1361183626" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10275060972625756754"><b>Okay, okay, where to start with this thing...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455047140ra/18048141.gif' width='500' height='260' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>***Enter Diplomatic Val***<br/><br/>*<br/>*<br/>*<br/><br/><i>
  <b>FUCK.</b>
</i> <br/><br/>THIS. <br/><br/>BOOK.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458234290ra/18460582.gif' width='550' height='309' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh, I'm sorry, did I say "Diplomatic Val?"<br/><br/>My bad. <br/><br/>Cause I tripped that bitch on her way in. <br/><br/>Now, don't get me wrong. I love me some Tillie Cole and I still will after this shit show. <br/><br/>But, as I was saying:<br/><br/><b>FUCK this book and the whispernet it came in on.</b><br/><br/><b>***Spoilers***<br/>***Spoilers***<br/>***Spoilers***<br/>***FUCKING***<br/>***Spoilers***<br/><br/>I <i>wish</i> I would have read some.</b><br/><br/>In all sincerity though, I'm about to fucking WRECK th</span>
  <span id="freeText10275060972625756754" style="display:none"><b>Okay, okay, where to start with this thing...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455047140ra/18048141.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>***Enter Diplomatic Val***<br><br>*<br>*<br>*<br><br><i>
  <b>FUCK.</b>
</i> <br><br>THIS. <br><br>BOOK.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458234290ra/18460582.gif" width="550" height="309" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, I'm sorry, did I say "Diplomatic Val?"<br><br>My bad. <br><br>Cause I tripped that bitch on her way in. <br><br>Now, don't get me wrong. I love me some Tillie Cole and I still will after this shit show. <br><br>But, as I was saying:<br><br><b>FUCK this book and the whispernet it came in on.</b><br><br><b>***Spoilers***<br>***Spoilers***<br>***Spoilers***<br>***FUCKING***<br>***Spoilers***<br><br>I <i>wish</i> I would have read some.</b><br><br>In all sincerity though, I'm about to fucking WRECK this thing for you. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447881696ra/17061364.gif" width="245" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So stop reading if you really want to read this book...<br> <br>...Or keep reading if you really want to avoid some major, unnecessary book depression of the highest order. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458234290ra/18460583.gif" width="500" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There: you've been warned. <br>So don't act like I pissed in your Cheerios if you read this and then wish you hadn't. <br><br>But if you DO feel that way?<br><br>#Twinsies<br><br>Cause that's how I feel after trudging through this thing. <br><br>How else do I feel?<br><br>Depressed. <br><br>And you know what? If I wanted to be depressed, I'd go to work.<br>Or watch <i>Beaches</i>. <br>Or <i>Titanic</i>. <br><br>Cause this book?<br><br>It's like someone took <i>A Walk to Remember</i>, <i>Sweet November</i>, <i>The Boy Who Snuck in My Bedroom Window</i>, and <i>The Fault in Our Stars</i>...wrote them all down on pink heart-shaped paper...<br><br><b>And stuck them in a mother effin' JAR of a thousand piss-me-the-fuck-offs.</b> <br><br>Now, I actually <i>liked</i> all of those previous books/movies.<br><br>With <i>Walk</i>, the whole chick-dies-at-the-end shtick hadn't really been done in that manner before and I read the book and went to the movie (as a hormone-addled teenager at the time, mind you) not really expecting that ending. <br><br>And with <i>Fault</i>, whelp it was kind of like <i>Titanic</i>. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458234290ra/18460584.gif" width="240" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You knew old girl wasn't gonna make it to port before you went in. <br><br>Whelp, with THIS shipwreck, I had no idea. <br><br>And being that a NON-HEA (because that's what this was in my salty opinion) has been unprecedented before in my experience with Tillie Cole - and being that an HEA is just something I EXPECT with something peddled as ROMANCE - I did NOT expect this outcome. <br><br>But believe me, you saw the writing on the goddamned wall early-ish on.<br><br>But only after you were knee deep in the story and had one of those halfway moments where you are like, "Well we are already halfway there so..."<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458235174ra/18460699.gif" width="500" height="387" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Might as well just keep on keepin' on. Ya'll.<br><br>And in ONE way, this WAS very much like Titanic. <br><br>Because why, you ask?<br><br>Because in this case...<br><br><b>The band was playing as the ship went down...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458235174ra/18460700.gif" width="500" height="278" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Whoops, wrong band.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458235174ra/18460701.gif" width="350" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There we go. <br>Nice job fellas.<br><br>*<br>*<br>*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458235174ra/18460701.gif" width="350" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oops, they're still going...<br><br>As I was.<br><br>Again, don't get me wrong. <br><br>This was very well written - if super sappy and somewhat cliche at times. <br>And I truly felt the connection between Rune and Poppy.<br>And I became attached to them, for sure. <br><br>But honestly, it was like watching that movie <i>Earth</i>.<br><br>They introduce you to the tres adorbs wild mama elephant and her baby elephant...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458237378ra/18461079.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...They even give them names and then take us along on their journey across the Sahara or some shit. <br><br>We get all attached...<br><br>And then these bastards show up:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458235830i/18460817.jpg" width="480" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And fucking turn baby elephant into dinner. <br><br>Now, tangent. <br><br>While searching for possible pics of said predator/prey moment, I came across some very graphic ones of lions attacking an elephant. <br>And it made me so upset, I can't even tell you. <br><br>So you're welcome for not putting one of those in here.<br><br>But I digress. <br><br>My point?<br><br>If I wanted to read about someone I'm attached to dying slowly of a horrible cancer and the effect that that has on their loved ones?<br><br>I would revisit all those super fun memories of my own 12 year-old self and the experience of watching my mother die in agony from said disease. <br><br>Or I could just make it faster and stab myself in the face with a sharp object. <br><br>Cause you know what? <br><br>As beautiful as this kind of story can be - and rightfully IS - to some people, it's just not what I would call a "good time." <br><br>I read to escape the daily grind and have fun, not to be reminded of the worst memories and feelings of my life. <br><br>Which is why I usually avoid books with death endings like the plague. <br><br>However, being that it's my practice not to read too many reviews of a book I am thinking about reading, as well as the fact that this wasn't alluded to in the blurb (I was legit expecting the oops I had your 15 year-old Oslo baby twist, no joke), I was simply not prepared for this book to...be this kind of book.<br><br>Needless to say, take this review with the proverbial grain of salt. <br><br>Most of my GR friends loved it, and for good reason. <br><br>It's well written - as all of Cole's book are, in my opinion - and I really did like Rune and Poppy (unrealistic and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manic_Pixie_Dream_Girl" rel="nofollow noopener">Manic Pixie Dream Girl</a> though she may may be).<br><br>Their love story was the epic "loved you since childhood" story that dreams are made of...<br><br><i>My</i> dreams though? <br>End with me and my hubster getting old and gray together.<br>Sitting on our front porch swing. <br>Yelling at the street kids to get the fuck off our front lawn.<br><br>NOT of my beloved soulmate dying of Cancer before age 30. And leaving me behind to experience a world I never want to experience: one without him in it. <br><br>And so with that...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443818905ra/16414849.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Find me at:<br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283577.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283578.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1480551788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5868602394997083012">This is by far my most favorite of the novels I have written. It called me to write it over 18 months ago, but I resisted until I could resist no more. Poppy and Rune have taken my entire heart and soul with them on this journey, and I am forever changed by it. Moved by it. Inspired by it.<br/><br/>I hope you all love this novel as much as I loved bringing these beautiful characters to life. <br/><br/>Yes, it's a tearjerker. But it's so much more too. Take a chance on this story of young, but undeniable love, you w</span>
  <span id="freeText5868602394997083012" style="display:none">This is by far my most favorite of the novels I have written. It called me to write it over 18 months ago, but I resisted until I could resist no more. Poppy and Rune have taken my entire heart and soul with them on this journey, and I am forever changed by it. Moved by it. Inspired by it.<br /><br />I hope you all love this novel as much as I loved bringing these beautiful characters to life. <br /><br />Yes, it's a tearjerker. But it's so much more too. Take a chance on this story of young, but undeniable love, you won't be sorry.<br /><br />Like Poppy says, "Always say yes to new adventures."<br /><br />Much love and happy reading.<br /><br />Tills xx<br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1580858904?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1580858904" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15630365323189686356"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 6 STARS!! ::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458146505i/18449755.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <strong>
    <em>Kiss eight hundred and nineteen was the kiss that changed it all. The kiss that proved that a long-haired brooding boy from Norway and a quirky girl from the Deep South could find a love to rival the greats.<br/><br/>It showed that love was simply the tenacity to make sure that the other half of your heart knew he, or she, was adored in every way. In every minute of every day. That love was tenderness in its purest form.</em>
  </strong>
</blockquote><br/>WOW. <strong>WOW.</strong> <strong>
  <em>WOW!!!!!!</em>
</strong><br/><br/>This </span>
  <span id="freeText15630365323189686356" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 6 STARS!! ::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458146505i/18449755.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <strong>
    <em>Kiss eight hundred and nineteen was the kiss that changed it all. The kiss that proved that a long-haired brooding boy from Norway and a quirky girl from the Deep South could find a love to rival the greats.<br><br>It showed that love was simply the tenacity to make sure that the other half of your heart knew he, or she, was adored in every way. In every minute of every day. That love was tenderness in its purest form.</em>
  </strong>
</blockquote><br>WOW. <strong>WOW.</strong> <strong>
  <em>WOW!!!!!!</em>
</strong><br><br>This was one of the most breathtakingly <em>beautiful</em> books I have EVER read in my entire life. HOLY FEELS. I cried my way through most of the book because almost every scene was filled with the most <em>intense and powerful emotions</em> you can imagine. The sheer, undying strength of the LOVE that Rune and Poppy shared overwhelmed me. <strong>
  I loved every single word of this book
</strong>. And the ending was absolutely <em>perfect</em> for their story. This is one of those books that I know will stay with me forever and ever. I loved it with all my heart and HIGHLY RECOMMEND it to everyone as my first 6 STAR RATING of the year!!!<br><br>I'm exhausted. I've slept barely 2 hours. After I washed all the mascara tear streaks from my face, I went to bed thinking about this book. I fell asleep thinking about this book. I woke up thinking about this book. I can't stop thinking about this book. I keep replaying the story, the beautiful quotes, the powerful scenes over and over in my head. I can't get over <em>how beautiful</em> this book was. If there has ever been a single book that has EVER made me believe that REAL LOVE truly lasts forever and ever, THIS IS IT.<br><br>This is what it's about...<br><blockquote>
  <em><strong> One kiss lasts a moment.<br>But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. </strong><br><br>One boy.<br>One girl.<br>A bond that is forged in an instant and cherished for a decade.<br>A bond that neither time nor distance can break.<br>A bond that will last forever.<br>Or so they believe.<br><br>When seventeen-year-old Rune Kristiansen returns from his native Norway to the sleepy town of Blossom Grove, Georgia, where he befriended Poppy Litchfield as a child, he has just one thing on his mind. Why did the girl who was one half of his soul, who promised to wait faithfully for his return, cut him off without a word of explanation?<br><br>Rune’s heart was broken two years ago when Poppy fell silent. When he discovers the truth, he finds that the greatest heartache is yet to come.</em>
</blockquote><br>For anyone who want/needs to know the ending, I've included everything in the hidden spoiler at the link below. You don't have to read it first, but I know many of you like to know. I personally always have to know. I knew everything in this spoiler before I read the book and honestly (just for me), knowing was what made me enjoy the book more because I had that lifeline and reassurance. It's totally up to you!<br><br>*** <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There are 3 questions I ask about every single book I ever read before I even dare consider reading: CHEATING?? TRIANGLE?? HEA??<br><br>Sometimes I ask other readers, sometimes I ask the author. In this case, the author approached me with her book so I got to chat with her about it and ask her my questions directly. I'm going to share her answers with you, because they were what made me go "OMG, I have to read this book!"<br><br>No cheating.<br>No triangle.<br>And here's the scoop on the HEA...<br><br>This is exactly what the author told me:<br><br><em>"The girl has cancer. She's terminal. The story is about how the boy helps her collect her 'boy kisses', a task given to her by her grandma when she was young. The task is to collect 1000 before she dies. The boy makes it his mission, before the girl passes, to get her all 1000.<br><br>The girl does pass, but the epilogue is set 10 years later, where he finds himself with her again in the afterlife--it's quite a spiritual ending, but beautiful. It gives a tearjerker ending, a HEA finish. The heaven sequence, reflects a theme that runs throughout the entire novel.<br><br>Hope that's ok! It is a weepy, that's the plain truth, but, to me, the epilogue makes it a HEA in its feel."</em><br>_____________________<br><br>Next, I asked her: One more question. Does he end up with another girl after she passes? Or was she it for him?<br><br>And she said: <em>She's it for him. Epic love story. Soulmates.I couldn't ever put him with anyone else. She is his everything. It would wound me if he'd got with anyone else! Again, the epilogue ensures they are meant to be forever.</em><br>______________________<br><br>Now that I've finished it myself, I can say that it totally felt HEA. At the end of the day, it doesn't matter WHERE they are -- whether they're on earth or maybe somewhere else -- as long as they are actually together and happy, and able to be together and happy for the rest of their 'time', then that's what makes the ending happy. The heaven sequence when they both found each other again genuinely felt HEA. It was like they'd found each other again and this time nothing could tear them apart.<br><br>It was like the ultimate confirmation that was almost MORE “HEA” than anything on earth because you knew that now, even death couldn't separate them anymore. It genuinely FELT HEA… like they'd found each other and were reunited for all of eternity.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ***<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <em>“She’s the love of my life. And I’m not walking away from her, even for a second.”</em>
</blockquote><br>HOLY INTENSITY. There was more raw emotion in the first few chapters of this book alone than in most entire books I've read. I had tears in my eyes, my heart was pounding in my throat, I felt like I couldn't breathe because of how <em>much</em> I was <em>feeling</em> for this book. I alternated between crying and almost crying, falling in love and feeling overjoyed for the beauty of their fierce love for each other, and feeling broken-hearted for everything they were going through.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>I held her. I held her so tightly I thought she would ask me to let go. But she didn’t, and I wouldn’t. I didn’t dare let go, in case when I lifted my head she wasn’t here.<br>I needed her to be here.<br>I needed her to stay.</em>
</blockquote><br>Every few chapters, I had to step away from the book to regain my composure. But even though I wanted to take breathers, I just as desperately <em>needed</em> to keep reading. I wanted more of their story while simultaneously wanting to stop time. No matter what, every time I picked the book back up again, I was crying within moments. On more than one occasion, I'd have to stop reading because I literally couldn't see the words any longer through my tears. AND I LOVED IT!! Could. Not. Stop. Reading.<br><br>I loved how much validity the author gave to young love. It's so often dismissed as 'you aren't ready yet' or 'you can't know what you want yet', but this book gave it <em>power</em> and <em>strength</em>. I'm a firm believer that you know when you fall in love -- forever love -- even if you find your soul mate when you're young.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>When he reached me, he didn’t touch the tear stains on my cheeks, as I left his untouched. Closing his eyes, he took my mouth in a kiss. And in this kiss I felt his outpourings of love. I felt a love, that at seventeen, I was blessed to have received.<br>A love that knew no boundaries.</em>
</blockquote><br>Poppy's strength was beyond powerful. And the fierce loyalty and strength with which Rune loved her was beyond intense. He loved this girl with all of his heart and soul and he was willing to do absolutely anything to make every moment of her life be filled with that love.<br><br>This book <em>needs</em> to be made into a movie. I could picture every scene so vividly in my mind as I read and it would easily make an incredible transition to screen. *sends up silent prayer to movie gods*<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>Then she promised, “My kisses are all yours. No one else will ever have these lips but you.”<br>I brushed my lips against her more time and echoed her words. “My kisses are all yours. No one will ever have these lips but you.”</em>
</blockquote><br>I highly recommend this book with all my heart. Be prepared to ugly cry. Possibly more than once. I can almost guarantee that you'll be full-out sobbing at some point. But know that it is absolutely worth every single tear... because the ending was more beautiful than I could ever have imagined.<br><br>Heart-breaking, breathtaking, unforgettable, and profoundly beautiful, this book will stay in my heart a long time to come. More than anything, it truly made me believe in undying love -- the kind of love that endures the most intense pain imaginable, and still shines through forever and ever and ever.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>“You’ll stay by my side, won’t you?”<br>Crouching down, I cupped her cheeks. “Forever.” </em>
</blockquote><br><b>RATING: 6 STARS!!! Standalone romance.</b><br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01CXYSEB2/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=aesbooblo-20&amp;linkId=a93f092d762d3491b02eefeb8e986d09" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Buy A THOUSAND BOY KISSES (Kindle)</a><br><br>__________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/subscribe/" rel="nofollow noopener">Subscribe by email</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1339817130" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1339817130" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1339817130?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2016-ya-challenge">2016-ya-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1339817130" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer304826922889338161"><b> ALL THE STARS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/4227C4D9-5E77-4FE0-9B53-9B60FB1C3942_zps6f5xbpej.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432854._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4227C4D9-5E77-4FE0-9B53-9B60FB1C3942_zps6f5xbpej.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Live hard, love harder. Chase dreams, seek adventures… capture moments. Live beautifully.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br/>Every once in a while, you read a book that completely turns your world upside down. It happens every so often, and when it does, your heart is so full you feel like it could burst. I wish I could express how much this book impacted me, how much I felt while I read it, but the words to convey just how wonderful it was aren’t going to be enough. I guess I could quote Tilli</span>
  <span id="freeText304826922889338161" style="display:none"><b> ALL THE STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/4227C4D9-5E77-4FE0-9B53-9B60FB1C3942_zps6f5xbpej.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432854._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4227C4D9-5E77-4FE0-9B53-9B60FB1C3942_zps6f5xbpej.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Live hard, love harder. Chase dreams, seek adventures… capture moments. Live beautifully.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br>Every once in a while, you read a book that completely turns your world upside down. It happens every so often, and when it does, your heart is so full you feel like it could burst. I wish I could express how much this book impacted me, how much I felt while I read it, but the words to convey just how wonderful it was aren’t going to be enough. I guess I could quote Tillie herself and say that this book is <b>as special as special can be </b>. It’s one of those rare books that I want to give all the stars too! I loved it so much. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/096CC5E1-A191-49C0-98AB-6206EA6B1775_zpscvdcb4w0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432855._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 096CC5E1-A191-49C0-98AB-6206EA6B1775_zpscvdcb4w0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tillie is a favorite of mine, and when I heard she had a new YA book coming out I jumped for joy! I love YA and I love her writing so I figured it would be a great read. I didn’t realize just how good it would be. I didn’t realize it would be the kind of book that moved me and captivated me. <br><br>Poppy and Rune meet when they are 5 years old. They are neighbors and they quickly become the best of friends. Poppy’s mamaw gives Poppy a jar when she’s just a kid. A jar to fill with kisses. 1000 boy kisses to be exact. Rune, even at a young age, decides he will be the one to give Poppy these kisses. It can’t be anyone else. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/6EBA8A44-1AB3-43AD-8E9A-1DC9D3891A81_zps3ywpspnu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432856._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6EBA8A44-1AB3-43AD-8E9A-1DC9D3891A81_zps3ywpspnu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Rune and Poppy spend their childhood together and in love. Rune ends up having no choice but to go to his native country of Norway and to do the unthinkable… leave Poppy behind. No matter how temporary he can’t imagine ever leaving his girl. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>This was Poppymin. the girl who would run to the blossom grove, laughing and dancing all the way… I couldn’t leave her. She couldn’t leave me. She needed me. I needed her. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i> No matter what this couple goes through, no separation, no silence, could ever stop them from being together. They were meant to be. <br><br>Rune and Poppy are both amazing characters. I loved Rune’s love and devotion for his Poppy. And Poppy… one of the best heroines I’ve ever read! She had the most fantastic attitude no matter what was happening in life. For such a young girl, she was someone I looked up to and admired. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/3AE85A25-7539-4DBB-8D11-22CE4E9DE67A_zpshyj4hjp3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432857._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3AE85A25-7539-4DBB-8D11-22CE4E9DE67A_zpshyj4hjp3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tillie Cole is one of my favorite authors. This is by far her best book yet. These two characters and their story are completely unforgettable. This story isn’t always easy to read. It’s not a light read. It’s heavy. I had tears rolling down my face more often than I did not. It was heartbreakingly beautiful, but by the end, I had the biggest smile on my face. I promise you it is worth every single tear you will shed. It isn’t a book you want to miss out on. This is going on that list of one of my top favorite books EVER! If you haven’t read it yet, don’t miss out! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Poppy and Rune. Two halves of the same whole.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/403E023F-5CD8-40F5-9B1C-7F800E630E9C_zpszg09p0um.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458031801i/18432858._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 403E023F-5CD8-40F5-9B1C-7F800E630E9C_zpszg09p0um.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="304826922889338161" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1405426282?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/22324639-a">A.</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1405426282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6557705327296324160"><b>DNF</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458588032i/18505772._SX540_.jpg' width='600' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I should really start reading spoilers before I start the book. But this is Tillie Cole so I one-clicked it without thinking.<br/><br/><b>I didn’t DNF this book because the writing was <i>bad</i>.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586853ra/18505554.gif' width='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>On the contrary. The writing was great. <br/><br/><b>I didn’t DNF it because I didn’t like the characters.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586853ra/18505555.gif' width='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The characters were awesome. I loved them both dearly and with all my heart.<br/><br/><b>I didn’t DNF it because I couldn’t connect to the story or the characters.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457030184ra/18311347.gif' width='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>No, the real reason is exactly the opposite. <br/><br/><b>I DNF'D IT BECAUSE I CONNECTED TO</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6557705327296324160" style="display:none"><b>DNF</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458588032i/18505772._SX540_.jpg" width="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I should really start reading spoilers before I start the book. But this is Tillie Cole so I one-clicked it without thinking.<br><br><b>I didn’t DNF this book because the writing was <i>bad</i>.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586853ra/18505554.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the contrary. The writing was great. <br><br><b>I didn’t DNF it because I didn’t like the characters.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586853ra/18505555.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The characters were awesome. I loved them both dearly and with all my heart.<br><br><b>I didn’t DNF it because I couldn’t connect to the story or the characters.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457030184ra/18311347.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No, the real reason is exactly the opposite. <br><br><b>I DNF'D IT BECAUSE I CONNECTED TOO MUCH.</b><br><br>I was one hundred percent invested into the story right until the 35% mark. And then BAM! <br><br>The three dreaded, ugly words....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586853ra/18505558.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I was done. I was so pissed I almost threw my tablet against the wall.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458586962ra/18505565.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because I can't stomach another book that will make me feel miserable for days after finishing it. And no ending will make me feel better, believe me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455619336ra/18125388.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Real life sometimes sucks. And I want to use my books as an escape from the harsh reality.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492124025i/22485193.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='300"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1336589526" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer628154984591112526"><b>*****10+++++++++ FOREVER ALWAYS TO INFINITY STARS*****</b><br/>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br/><br/><br/><b>As I stared at Rune, I asked myself how I had gotten so lucky. I was loved by this boy, loved so fiercely that other loves paled in comparison.<br/><br/>I closed my eyes and replayed our lives in my mind. I remembered the times I hugged him and he hugged me harder. I remembered how I kissed him and he kissed me deeper. And best of all, I remembered how I would love him and he would always strive to love me more. </b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/1cea56023860a765c70596f235e01e81_zpspkuuqof5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457925295i/18422827._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 1cea56023860a765c70596f235e01e81_zpspkuuqof5.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>W</span>
  <span id="freeText628154984591112526" style="display:none"><b>*****10+++++++++ FOREVER ALWAYS TO INFINITY STARS*****</b><br>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br><br><br><b>As I stared at Rune, I asked myself how I had gotten so lucky. I was loved by this boy, loved so fiercely that other loves paled in comparison.<br><br>I closed my eyes and replayed our lives in my mind. I remembered the times I hugged him and he hugged me harder. I remembered how I kissed him and he kissed me deeper. And best of all, I remembered how I would love him and he would always strive to love me more. </b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/1cea56023860a765c70596f235e01e81_zpspkuuqof5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457925295i/18422827._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1cea56023860a765c70596f235e01e81_zpspkuuqof5.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Where do I begin to describe this incredible story???<br>Firstly, I’d like to give Tillie Cole a <b>BILLION GIRL KISSES</b> for creating the most beautiful love story I have read….<b>EVER!!!</b> I’d like to follow that up by stating that I also have a bone to pick with her because how can anything I read after this measure up!!??? I seriously don’t think it’s possible! This, in my honest opinion, is Tillie Cole’s <u>
  <b>MASTERPIECE</b>
</u>. She has always been one of my top favorite authors, but after having read this GORGEOUS &amp; HEARTBREAKING story, Tillie has definitely earned her place as my <b>#1 FAVORITE AUTHOR!</b> <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/18420559._SY540__zpskm0zlmda.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457922297i/18422512.jpg" alt=" photo 18420559._SY540__zpskm0zlmda.jpg" width="365" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I knew even before I read this book that it was YA, and I don’t have anything against this genre, but I mostly read NA and Adult Contemporary books. That being said, I think those of you who tend to steer clear from YA really need to forego that stance and pick this one up ASAP! Rune and Poppy are two of the most endearing and wonderful characters you will ever come across in your reading adventures. Their love for each other was so awe inspiring and it will make you wish that a love like this could come into your lives.<br><br>Tillie’s writing is beyond exquisite. I highlighted so much of this book and found it so hard to pick just one quote to add to my review. There were some quotes that were so breathtaking but to post them here, would possibly spoil the story and you definitely need to go into this one blind.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/18420558._SX540__zpsjozbpabl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457922297i/18422513.jpg" alt=" photo 18420558._SX540__zpsjozbpabl.jpg" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>If I could shout it from the rooftops I would say - <i>
  <b>”Drop whatever book you are reading and pick this one up!!”</b>
</i> Make sure you have a box of tissues handy because the tears will start freely flowing!! Also download the song <i>
  <b>”If I Could Fly”</b>
</i> by One Direction. It is mentioned in the book and it gave me goosebumps while I was reading this amazing book.<br><br><br>This is definitely my <b>FAVORITE</b> Tillie Cole creation and this story is one I will carry in my heart for a long time to come. <b>BEST OF 2016! BEST BOOK EVER!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452041283i/17638294.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1579336749" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579336749" />
    <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin"><img alt="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603831478p2/17438949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1579336749?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin">Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/29504138-a-thousand-boy-kisses">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579336749" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6751155287080195468"><b>THIS. BOOK. BROKE. MY. HEART. INTO. A. THOUSAND. LITTLE. HEARTS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465480303ra/19362799.gif' alt=' ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I didn't think I would make it through this book. I cried and cried and cried and ............ <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465480303ra/19362800.gif' alt=' ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480303i/19362801._SY540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is a love story like no other and I hate/love it. God! Whyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy!!!!! What can I say to you people out there! My feelings are just shot! This book is so beautiful, so sad and just damn it. <br/><br/>Rune and Poppy met when they were 5 years old. Rune had just moved from Norway to Georgia and he hated it until that moment he met P</span>
  <span id="freeText6751155287080195468" style="display:none"><b>THIS. BOOK. BROKE. MY. HEART. INTO. A. THOUSAND. LITTLE. HEARTS.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465480303ra/19362799.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't think I would make it through this book. I cried and cried and cried and ............ <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465480303ra/19362800.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480303i/19362801._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a love story like no other and I hate/love it. God! Whyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy!!!!! What can I say to you people out there! My feelings are just shot! This book is so beautiful, so sad and just damn it. <br><br>Rune and Poppy met when they were 5 years old. Rune had just moved from Norway to Georgia and he hated it until that moment he met Poppy and everything became crystal clear. He met his best friend, his soul mate. But nothing lasts forever and I sure didn't see this one coming. I had my mind set on not finishing the book because I thought when they were separated at 15 that it would be just another "oh they are apart now and lets find other people and this was all meaningless". It wasn't like that, not like that at all. Did I mention is was the most beautifully, sad love story ever! <br><br><b>EXCERPT<br><br>"Rune," she said, her voice serious and strong, "you live right next door, and you're a Viking and I just love Vikings. I think we should be best friends."<br>"Best friends?" I asked. <br>Poppy nodded her head and pushed her hand further toward me. Slowly reaching out my own hand, I gripped hold of hers and gave it two shakes, like she'd shown me. <br>A handshake. <br>"So now we are best friends?" I asked, as Poppy pulled her hand back. <br>"Yes!" she said excitedly. "Poppy and Rune." She brought her finger to her chin and looked up. Her lips stuck out again, like she was thinking very hard. "It sounds good, don't you think? 'Poppy and Rune, best friends for infinity!'"</b><br><br>Just kill me now because you all have no idea!!!!!!!!!!!! :-(<br><br>So Poppy's mamaw died when Poppy was 8 and she left Poppy and mason jar with little hearts in them so she could collect a thousand special boy kisses. She was to write them down on the hearts and have them for a lifetime to pass down to her children. <br><br>Rune and Poppy were in the blossom grove, Rune was comforting Poppy. Then Poppy told Rune about the jar her mamaw gave to her. <br><br><b>EXCERPT<br><br>He stared down at me, then at the jar. My chest hurt again; I could see he wasn't happy by the look on his face. He'd gone all moody again. <br>I stepped closer to my best friend, and Rune's eyes fixed on mine. <br>"Poppymin," he said, his voice deeper-hard and strong. "Poppymin! It means my Poppy. For infinity, forever and always. You're MY Poppy!"<br>I opened my mouth to shout back at him, to tell him this was an adventure I just had to start. But as I did, Rune leaned forward and suddenly pressed his lips to mine. <br>I froze. I couldn't move a muscle as I felt his lips against my lips. They were warm. He tasted like cinnamon. The wind blew his long hair over my cheeks. It started to tickle my nose. <br>Rune pulled back, but his face stayed near mine. I tried to breathe, but my chest felt funny, kind of light and fluffy. And my heart was beating so fast. So fast that I pressed my hand over my chest to feel it racing underneath. <br><br>•••••<br><br>"You kissed me," I whispered, stunned. Rune lifted his hand to hold mine. He lowered our joined hands by his side. <br>"I'll give you a thousand kisses, Poppymin. All of them. No one will kiss you ever, but me."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480303i/19362802.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story tells about Rune's love for photography and how he was going to college in New York because of said photography. Poppy played the cello and was going to college in New York because of said cello. They were going to be together living their dreams. They had friends, they had each other, they had a love that could match no other. And then... I will never tell you but for the love of all that is holy, it all changed and it's the most heart breaking thing I have read in a long time! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480303i/19362803._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending was so sad, I can't even. I just can't!!!!!!! Rune and Poppy's story ends in the blossom grove. My word of advice is to have a box of kleenex handy. I almost went through a whole box myself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480487i/19362826.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465480487i/19362827._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you love unbelievable love stories, because there can't be love like that in this crappy world, then this story is for you. If you don't really want your heart broken and stomped on then it's probably not, but read it anyway! <br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/06/a-thousand-boy-kisses-by-tillie-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6751155287080195468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1577341681" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577341681" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577341681?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577341681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3141312626256387256">If I could give this book a million stars I would. It’s legit one of my favorite reads of all time. I love Tillie Cole, but I’ll be honest I wasn’t expecting a book like this from her. I mean I love all her books, no matter what she is writing, so why I painted her in a box is beyond me. I mean I first fell in love with her writing in <i>Sweet Home</i>. Then I met her at a signing and put together that she had also written one of my favorite MC series, I know I am dense for not realizing this sooner. T</span>
  <span id="freeText3141312626256387256" style="display:none">If I could give this book a million stars I would. It’s legit one of my favorite reads of all time. I love Tillie Cole, but I’ll be honest I wasn’t expecting a book like this from her. I mean I love all her books, no matter what she is writing, so why I painted her in a box is beyond me. I mean I first fell in love with her writing in <i>Sweet Home</i>. Then I met her at a signing and put together that she had also written one of my favorite MC series, I know I am dense for not realizing this sooner. Then I read <i>Raze</i> and let me tell you, I LOVED THAT BOOK, I MEAN LOVED IT! That series has been my favorite from Tillie, until now. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457928238i/18423053._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rune and Poppy meet when they are five years old. Rune is from Norway and has a chip on his shoulder, even at five. Poppy is this fiery girl who already has this amazing love for life. She introduces herself to Rune and he is never the same, they are never the same.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457928238i/18423054._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At eight, Poppy’s grandmother gives her a jar of hearts that she is to fill with her most amazing, epic, meaningful kisses. Her new adventure is to obtain a thousand of these unique kisses in her life. Rune decides to claim all her kisses since no other guy will ever have his Poppy. <br><br>This story is YA so your first thought might be that their connection or love may be immature, that couldn’t be farther from the truth. I never got that vibe from Poppy and Rune. Despite their age, I felt their undeniable love from the beginning and it never let up. Their love story is something to be admired, I would go as far to say I would like to model some of myself after Poppy and Rune. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457928238i/18423055._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book just made me think and it made me feel if you have read my reviews for long I love a book that makes me want to change. I think we all have room for improvement in life. Like most people I want to be the best person I can be and this book reminded me that life is worth living. That love was worth the risk. That people deserve forgiveness and second chances. That true love is forever and unconditional. <br><br><i>A Thousand Boy Kisses</i> is unique and I loved every minute. I loved the insane amount of emotions I felt because it means I was truly connected to the story and characters. Poppy and Rune are some of my favorite characters of all time and I won’t be forgetting them anytime soon. I have read over a thousand books in just a few years and I am sure I will read a thousand more, but I can promise you I will never forget this story. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457928238i/18423056._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br><i>Teasers created by me with stock images purchased from depositphotos.</i><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1857547864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1857547864" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1857547864?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=strong-female-characters">strong-female-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=published-in-2016">published-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=young-adult-contemporary">young-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1857547864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer388592115077532784"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Tillie Cole is a new-to-me author. I have heard a lot of great things about her books and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25912358.A_Thousand_Boy_Kisses' title='A Thousand Boy Kisses by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Thousand Boy Kisses</a> is one of them. The cover is so beautiful as well as the title. I must say though that I wasn't prepared for its intensity and heaviness. The moment I started it, I knew it would be a challenging book to read because of its melancholy tone. It sure was. The story was more poignant than I've expected.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Maybe we're like a cherry blossom, Rune. Like shooting stars. Maybe w</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText388592115077532784" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br>Tillie Cole is a new-to-me author. I have heard a lot of great things about her books and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25912358.A_Thousand_Boy_Kisses" title="A Thousand Boy Kisses by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Thousand Boy Kisses</a> is one of them. The cover is so beautiful as well as the title. I must say though that I wasn't prepared for its intensity and heaviness. The moment I started it, I knew it would be a challenging book to read because of its melancholy tone. It sure was. The story was more poignant than I've expected.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Maybe we're like a cherry blossom, Rune. Like shooting stars. Maybe we loved too much too young and burned so bright that we had to fade out."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Rune Erik Kristiansen</b> and <b>Poppy Litchfield</b> have been best of friends since they were kids. Their friendship started when Rune and his family left their roots in Norway and started their lives in the U.S. He didn't want to live in the new country where it required him to speak English and adapt to the culture, but when he met the beautiful and bubbly child Poppy, his feelings changed. The two of them grew up and somehow developed a much deeper relationship as the year went by. Poppy, whose grandmother passed away, grew up with a goal in life to collect a thousand boy kisses. It's an idea left by her grandma to her. Each time she gets a kiss from her special boy, the details should be written in a pink heart and be placed in a jar. The boy kisses, of course, were given by Rune.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's okay to laugh. It's okay to smile. It's okay to feel happy. Or what's the point in life?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This book is a real heartbreaker. It actually reminded me of those books I've read in the past that made me cry a river (I won't mention any title because it would be a spoiler). I was able to connect with the story. However, I failed to appreciate it even more because of its <b>predictability</b>. I knew exactly what's about to come even before the 'twist' in the early part of the book happened. I wasn't surprised when Poppy finally revealed why she went away and didn't communicate with Rune anymore.<br><br>Also, <b>lots and lots of cheese were thrown everywhere</b>. I couldn't even count the number of sappy dialogues and scenes. For me, they are a little bit exaggerated. Not to mention how their conversations slowly became repetitive each chapter.<br><br>Despite the flaws I've mentioned, the ending somehow moved me. I was blown away by the things that happened. Of course I knew at the back of my mind that their story would end that way, but still, I wasn't prepared for it. There was still a small part of me that longed for a different ending. A twist, perhaps. A Thousand Boy Kisses, as a whole, was a highly emotional YA love story. It's a book that touches the soul and makes you realize a lot of things in life. If you love heavy, angsty, and heartbreaking books, then this book is the one that you should devour. Just prepare lots and lots of tissues. You will really need them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="388592115077532784" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer11033926269408460491"><b>2.5 'Moonbeam hearts and sunshine smiles' </b><br/><br/>So on this <b>Mega Tuesday</b>, with political shit being flung at me from every direction - instead of an '<b>I voted</b>' sticker, perhaps mine should reflect the following sentiment.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458085277i/18442475.jpg' width='400' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Because, <i>A Thousand Boy Kisses</i> did not thaw this chick. I get it, I see how this read could get those tear ducts working, tug at those heart strings - its an emotional topic. But somewhere along the way, my disconnect button was hit, and I just didn't feel it. The characters were odd, a</span>
  <span id="freeText11033926269408460491" style="display:none"><b>2.5 'Moonbeam hearts and sunshine smiles' </b><br><br>So on this <b>Mega Tuesday</b>, with political shit being flung at me from every direction - instead of an '<b>I voted</b>' sticker, perhaps mine should reflect the following sentiment.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458085277i/18442475.jpg" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because, <i>A Thousand Boy Kisses</i> did not thaw this chick. I get it, I see how this read could get those tear ducts working, tug at those heart strings - its an emotional topic. But somewhere along the way, my disconnect button was hit, and I just didn't feel it. The characters were odd, and the dialogue just felt strange, these were 17 year old kids... I'm sorry, I just don't buy it. I guess my cynicism is showing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458085738ra/18442504.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That said, I'm a fan of Tillie's work - but this story just wasn't for me. Maybe if I had read it before some of its predecessors, for example - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11870085.The_Fault_in_Our_Stars" title="The Fault in Our Stars by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fault in Our Stars</a> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I would have felt different. But if this one has caught your eye, don't let my opinion sway you, it's been getting lots of love - so hopefully you will join the majority, and love it too. Unfortunately for me, I didn't. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458086053ra/18442548.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1370387616" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1370387616?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=big-girl-panties-read">big-girl-panties-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=march-2016">march-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1370387616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1146487192129978436"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release date: </b> March 14 , 2016<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457997416i/18430278._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is one of <i>those</i> books. The ones that are special, the ones that stand out in your mind when you think about the books that impacted you the most. There is no doubt in my mind that years from now, I will remember these characters with crystal clarity. I can count on one hand the books that have tore me apart and demolished my peace of mind like this one. There really is no adequate w</span>
  <span id="freeText1146487192129978436" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release date: </b> March 14 , 2016<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457997416i/18430278._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is one of <i>those</i> books. The ones that are special, the ones that stand out in your mind when you think about the books that impacted you the most. There is no doubt in my mind that years from now, I will remember these characters with crystal clarity. I can count on one hand the books that have tore me apart and demolished my peace of mind like this one. There really is no adequate way to explain what you're in for when you step inside Poppy and Rune's world. <br><br>It's a world filled with kisses that make your heart burst. <br>Moonbeam hearts and sunshine smiles.<br>Best friends and soulmates who belong in each other's arms.<br>A boy and a girl who burn bright and blindingly beautiful together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458000201ra/18430461.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is so much to say about this book, but to tell you anything about where they take you and what you see would be doing a huge disservice to the author and what she created in this story. It would diminish the impact of what you are meant to feel, which is a million different things or more. <br><br>When I opened up A Thousand Boy Kisses, I believed I would be reading a simple and most likely sweet story about young love. Well, take the simple out of the equation, and add deep and impactful to your expectations because it's so much more than what you've bargained for. Tillie Cole is the kind of author who writes in a way that reaches inside of you and compels you to listen. Every book of hers I read, it solidifies my admiration for her ability to carry me away so effortlessly. For those few hours I'm lost inside her story, all I can do is turn the pages and attempt to contain my emotions. <br><br>Poppy was a heroine with an exquisitely pure heart. She was unique, carefree, and was much wiser than her years. She reveled in finding the joy in each and every moment and seeing the beauty that the world has to offer.<br><br><b>She'd always seen more going on in the world than anyone else I knew. She saw the light piercing the dark. She saw the good through the bad.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457999957ra/18430444.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rune met Poppy as a little boy when he moved next door to her. From the moment he set eyes on her everything clicked into place and the world rearranged itself around them. <br><br><b>We were only fifteen, but since the day I kissed her in the blossom grove, aged eight, there had never been anyone else.</b><br><br>They were inseparable.<br>Until they weren't anymore. <br><br>What happens afterward will leaving you gasping for your next breath. I'm not going to sit here and tell you this was an easy book to read. But when I turned that last page I was filled with indescribable emotion. And I was left in a place of contentment and peace and a desire to see the world through Poppy's eyes. Wishing to wring fulfillment and joy from every day, every hour, and every minute. <br><br>This book is categorized YA, but the themes and the mature characters make it feel like anything but. Even those who don't typically read this genre will get so much out of this book, I highly recommend it to anyone looking for something that will hit you on a visceral level. You'll get exactly what you're hoping for.<br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter"         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1337773113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer71883059103252512">★★★ <b>3 Stars</b> ★★★<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457957014i/18425593._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A Thousand Boy Kisses is a really sweet story about two childhood friends who are meant to be. Poppy and Rune meet when they are just five years old and have a beautiful and tender relationship.<br/><br/>When Poppy is eight years old, her grandmother gives her a jar full of plain pink hearts, and tells her to record all her boy kisses, but only the special ones, the ones that make her heart almost burst.<br/><br/>Poppy knows that Rune is the only boy she ever wants to kiss, and so she goes about fill</span>
  <span id="freeText71883059103252512" style="display:none">★★★ <b>3 Stars</b> ★★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457957014i/18425593._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A Thousand Boy Kisses is a really sweet story about two childhood friends who are meant to be. Poppy and Rune meet when they are just five years old and have a beautiful and tender relationship.<br><br>When Poppy is eight years old, her grandmother gives her a jar full of plain pink hearts, and tells her to record all her boy kisses, but only the special ones, the ones that make her heart almost burst.<br><br>Poppy knows that Rune is the only boy she ever wants to kiss, and so she goes about filling that jar with some very special moments.<br><br>I loved the first part of the book when Rune first arrives in America from Norway feeling angry that he has been taken away from his home, and then meeting his next door neighbour, the sweet and adorable Poppy. I even loved it when Rune turned bad boy for a little bit, albeit only a short while.<br><br>The plot twist does come quite early on in the book, and had I known it was going to go in that direction, I'll be honest and say I probably wouldn't have picked it up willingly. For this reason, I disconnected myself from the story a little, and didn't feel the huge emotional tug that a lot of readers are raving about. Poppy made a lot of decisions that I didn't quite understand and I was left feeling a bit confused at the lack of communication at times.<br><br>Overall, I liked it and thought that the love between the two was super cute, but a bit cheesy for my preference. <br><br><b>A Thousand Boy Kisses is a Young Adult Romance, told in dual POV</b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an <b>honest</b> review</i><br><br>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1369762116?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
