        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=march-2016">march-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369762116" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15490442360550294133"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release Date: </b> 15 March, 2016<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars <br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457778515i/18402556.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Write down where you were when you were kissed. You'll have a treasure jar of all the precious kisses that made your heart soar. </b><br/><br/>Tillie Cole is one of my favorite authors. She’s absolutely and wonderfully skilled at winning me over with her stories. I think she has some secret ninja skills that help her play with my emotions an</span>
  <span id="freeText15490442360550294133" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release Date: </b> 15 March, 2016<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars <br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457778515i/18402556.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Write down where you were when you were kissed. You'll have a treasure jar of all the precious kisses that made your heart soar. </b><br><br>Tillie Cole is one of my favorite authors. She’s absolutely and wonderfully skilled at winning me over with her stories. I think she has some secret ninja skills that help her play with my emotions and tug at my heartstrings. She just made me weep for hours and hours. I think my eyes are still a little bit puffy. Now I desperately need someone to hug me! My poor, poor heart.. <br><br>How to describe the experience of reading A Thousand Boy Kisses without giving away everything? I’m not sure I’m capable of that! I feel like I’m a second away from bursting and spilling EVERY. SINGLE. DETAIL. That book just made me feel so much and I have this strange urge to share all of thoughts and feelings it had evoked. <br><br>On the other hand, I would commit a serious bookish crime if I decided to spoil this story for you. It’s best to go into Poppy and Rune’s world without any additional knowledge (beside what was mentioned in the blurb) and slowly sink into this romantic, poignant coming of age story. So although I’m itching to write more about them I will not overshare (though it seriously kills me!).<br><br><b> One kiss lasts a moment.<br>But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457778515i/18402557.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the main characters. Seeing them grow, fall in love, share their ups and downs, it was all an amazing experience. The Dual point of view helped me understand Poppy and Rune better, it also made this story richer, more intricate and mixed with Tillie’s fabulous writing, it was a complete winner. I think I highlighted most of the book. <br><br><b> "It was so special that my heart almost burst." </b><br><br>A Thousand Boy Kisses is a special story and will definitely stay with me for a long while. It’s a young adult novel (I rarely read them anymore), but at the same time it’s very complex and mature (don’t be afraid to give it a chance just because you consider YA novels to be juvenile/frustrating/immature); <br><br>In this case the book is sweet and heart melting where it needs to be, and completely wrecking, gritty and angsty in other parts. <br><br>Tillie once again managed to mix sweetness with real hard life and created something so vivid, true and meaningful that I am still very much trembling from the emotions overload. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457778515i/18402558.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ‘Rune pressed a kiss just below my ear and whispered, “Sleep, baby. I got you.” And he did. He had me. Just like I had him.’ </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427385833i/14267472._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/?zx=1f57d632ff8fa1c8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Blog" <div id="review_1361214879" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1361214879" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1361214879?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=beautiful-cover">beautiful-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-fictional-boyfriends">my-fictional-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-favorite-book-ever">my-favorite-book-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=book-husband">book-husband</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1361214879" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9976514927313353541"><b> A THOUSAND Cherry Blossom Stars************************</b><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review)</i><br/><br/> <i>"Moonbean hearts and sunshine smiles"</i><br/><br/>The beauty of this novel consumed me. Tillie Cole once again takes ownership of my heart with her talent. She wrote a book entirely about love and how powerful and healing it could be. A magnificent story that will stay with me forever. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps728lhcnn.jpeg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpswu1eoqd1.jpeg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>I've been a loyal fan of Tillie Cole for years; I've read all of her books. I've always admired h</span>
  <span id="freeText9976514927313353541" style="display:none"><b> A THOUSAND Cherry Blossom Stars************************</b><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review)</i><br><br> <i>"Moonbean hearts and sunshine smiles"</i><br><br>The beauty of this novel consumed me. Tillie Cole once again takes ownership of my heart with her talent. She wrote a book entirely about love and how powerful and healing it could be. A magnificent story that will stay with me forever. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps728lhcnn.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457901246i/18420558._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps728lhcnn.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpswu1eoqd1.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457901246i/18420559._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpswu1eoqd1.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I've been a loyal fan of Tillie Cole for years; I've read all of her books. I've always admired her ability to always create new and different types of stories. She doesn't follow a recipe, and she's always captivated me with every single one.<br><br>I must admit that when I first started reading I wasn't sure I was actually going to love this book. As a blogger, unfortunately, I don't always get to pick what I want to read next. I usually have to read what's next on the calendar, always following a deadline. I was very frustrated with myself because while I recognized the stunning writing and characters, I wasn't connecting with the story. I simply blamed it on my mood. Then... at around 70% into the story, it finally happened, Tillie's magic finally reached into my heart and the feels, and tears were unstoppable.<br><br>Poppy and Rune's story is very powerful and inspiring. Reading this book truly feels like being kissed by a thousand kisses, your heart will burst!!! You can run and you can hide but it will catch up to you. I won't lie, it will tear your heart apart. You will cry and get goosebumps as you read one of the most beautiful love stories ever. <br><br>Love life even when you feel like it doesn't love you back. Love is all around us. Love and be loved, intently and purely. Love can change and heal anything and anybody. I believe it. <br><br><br>Thank you, author Tillie Cole for writing this stunning novel. <i>A Thousand Boy Kisses</i> will forever be one of my favorite books <b>EVER!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>My <i> A Thousand Boy Kisses</i> music playlist:<br>*Everyone's Got Something by Perrin Lamb<br>*Between Us by Peter Bradley Adams <br>*The Crazy Ones by Paloma Faith <br>* What We Leave Behind by Labrinth <br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453830803i/17878407.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1339880439" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1339880439" />
    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1339880439?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=feel-good-sweet">feel-good-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=i-m-an-angst-whore">i-m-an-angst-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=sweet-n-lovable-guys">sweet-n-lovable-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1339880439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3770271808289138800"><b>5 <i>'as special as special can be.'</i> STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Sometimes all we get are moments. There are no do-overs."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Yes, this is YA, not usually something I’ll read but it's also Tillie Cole. She gave me the Carillo boys, The Hades Hangmen and the Scarred Souls so it was a no-brainer for me. I had to read it, genre be damned! And seriously, so glad that I did. This was like nothing Tillie’s ever done before; this book is now among my favourites of hers. <br/><br/><b>“Poppy and Rune – there was no beginning to us and no end</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3770271808289138800" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>'as special as special can be.'</i> STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes all we get are moments. There are no do-overs."</i>
</b><br><br>Yes, this is YA, not usually something I’ll read but it's also Tillie Cole. She gave me the Carillo boys, The Hades Hangmen and the Scarred Souls so it was a no-brainer for me. I had to read it, genre be damned! And seriously, so glad that I did. This was like nothing Tillie’s ever done before; this book is now among my favourites of hers. <br><br><b>“Poppy and Rune – there was no beginning to us and no end.”</b><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/ATBK2_zpsny5krlrx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457905826i/18421098._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo ATBK2_zpsny5krlrx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is a tale about two teenagers, Poppy Litchfield and Rune Kristiansen, who have been best friends since the tender age of 5. They have a connection that many dream of and their bond captures the purest and deepest of friendship, love, trust, forgiveness and forever. <br><br><b>“She was my cherry blossom...unrivaled beauty…”</b><br><a href="http://imgur.com/QrxLnGy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457904856ra/18421000.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story is sweet, innocent, moving and full on tearjerker! Seriously, do not attempt without tissues.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/ip0rr6u" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457904856ra/18421001.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tillie took me on a achingly heartbreaking but also breathtakingly beautiful story that’s couched on the premise of Poppy’s jar of a thousand boy kisses. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/3vGAyF6" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457904856ra/18421002.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Upon her mamaw’s deathbed, she gifts Poppy with a jar of 1,000 blank, pink paper hearts and tasks her with recording all her boy kisses that <b><i>“make her heart almost burst, the ones that are the most special, the ones you want to remember…The ones that will make you smile when you remember them in your mind.”</i><br><a href="http://imgur.com/AiSHTL0" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450149243ra/17385776.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>“I’ll give you a thousand kisses, <i>Poppymin</i>. All of them. No one will kiss you ever, but me.”<br>“That would be forever, Rune. To never be kissed by anyone else means we’ll be together forever, and ever and ever!”</b><br><br>This story evoked a wide range of emotions from me and despite how hard or sad it was at times, Tillie managed to still give me a stunningly satisfying story about a truly epic love that touched me to the bottom of my heart. <br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/ATBK_zpsbq2stc7l.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457732726i/18396789._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ATBK_zpsbq2stc7l.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“My kisses are all yours, Rune. No one else will ever have these lips but you.”</b><br><br>I can’t recommend this book enough!!<br>If you love Tillie Cole, <b>read it.</b> <br>If you want an epic love story, <b>read it.</b> <br>If you want an unforgettable tale that will break you and put you back together again, <b>read it!</b> <br><a href="http://imgur.com/ENX3Ofy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457904856ra/18421003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>**ARC generously provided by author in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b> <br><a href="http://tiedupinromance.blogspot.be/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456487234i/18240613.png" width="400" height="148" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1724357324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1724357324" />
    <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth"><img alt="Beth Hudspeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495723320p2/18107143.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1724357324?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth Hudspeth" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth">Beth Hudspeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=book-reviews">book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1724357324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12043509253916858409"><b>Reviewed by</b>: <a href='https://hellobeautifulbookblog.com/2016/08/18/book-review-a-thousand-boy-kisses-by-tillie-cole/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>A Young Adult tearjerker romance that left me feeling more emotional for my lost time than for any of the characters. Sappy moments and over the top cheese just had me wishing it was over.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I’m not going into too much depth with this one because I don’t want to go off on a rant or something. I don’t like being negative. So many people have loved this book and I’m just really sad I couldn’t. I started out expecting to love this book. I love tearjerkers and </span>
  <span id="freeText12043509253916858409" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by</b>: <a href="https://hellobeautifulbookblog.com/2016/08/18/book-review-a-thousand-boy-kisses-by-tillie-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br /><br /><b>
  <i>A Young Adult tearjerker romance that left me feeling more emotional for my lost time than for any of the characters. Sappy moments and over the top cheese just had me wishing it was over.</i>
</b><br /><br />I’m not going into too much depth with this one because I don’t want to go off on a rant or something. I don’t like being negative. So many people have loved this book and I’m just really sad I couldn’t. I started out expecting to love this book. I love tearjerkers and I love YA romance. I have loved books like this in the past. I just didn’t feel a connection with this book at all. I had maybe one moment in the book that I liked and that was the story about God that I had heard before.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Live hard, love harder. Chase dreams, seek adventures … capture moments. Live beautifully.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Am I just not in the mood for cheese? I don’t know. I like some cheese, but I just felt like the characters were so unrealistic. The characters did not think or speak like teenagers and were just portrayed in a strange way. It seemed like the more I read of their dialogues, the more I felt this way. It was far fetched to say the least. I don’t mind far fetched plots. I love them from time to time, but where I draw the line are the characters. The characters in books I read must be realistic and straightforward. I love raw characters who you can absolutely fall in love with because of their honesty. That’s the characters I look for in books. I didn’t feel that connection one time in this book.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Why be miserable when you can be happy? It’s an obvious choice to me.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Okay enought with the negative. There were still some things I liked or found fascinating. Rune and Poppy are such unique names. I loved all the name choices. Grandma was so sad, but that was such a wonderful part of the story, a part I found very unique. The “Boy Kisses” piece was a mystery to me until Grandma explained. The idea of the love being contained in a jar for you to remember for your entire life is so sweet to me. I wonder if that was something Tillie Cole’s family came up with or some kind of tradition she had heard of or if it was all in her head. I liked the idea behind the story.<br /><br />I’m sorry guys for going all negative, but this was just too sappy, cheesy and completely unrealistic. I did not get emotional in the slightest. I did not connect. I also felt like this was a knock off of a couple of other books just put together.<br />I wanted to like this, but I just couldn’t. Thanks for bearing with me for my unpopular opinion.<br /><br /> <br /><br />Kiss #1<br /><br />With my love by the train tracks… I felt like my heart would burst.<br /><br />************<br /><br />Make me cry Tillie Cole, I dare you.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12043509253916858409" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br/><br/><b>TITLE:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br/><b>AUTHOR:</b> Tillie Cole <br/><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> March 15th, 2016<br/><br/><b>MY RATING</b><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=24vidfq' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i> One kiss lasts a moment.<br/>But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. </i>
</b><br/><br/><b>ONE THOUSAND BOY KISSES </b> We're first introduced to these two (Rune & Poppy) at the age of 5. Rune has just moved into th</span>
  <span id="freeText4792972141313434576" style="display:none"><b>༺**Complimentary Copy**༺</b> Provided by the author<br><b>"Tillie Cole"</b> in exchange for an honest review..Thank you!!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=24lsdp0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457581781i/18376882._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=4pwpli" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457416560i/18355902._SY540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> A Thousand Boy Kisses<br><b>AUTHOR:</b> Tillie Cole <br><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> March 15th, 2016<br><br><b>MY RATING</b><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=24vidfq" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457581781i/18376883.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Such a powerful, bittersweet, emotional, love story of epic proportions.</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=9gee8o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457514444i/18367276._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> One kiss lasts a moment.<br>But a thousand kisses can last a lifetime. </i>
</b><br><br><b>ONE THOUSAND BOY KISSES </b> We're first introduced to these two (Rune &amp; Poppy) at the age of 5. Rune has just moved into the neighborhood and living right next door to a girl. These two unlikely characters strike up an unusual friendship from the moment they met. She loves to play the cello and he loves to capture moments on film. <br>She thought he looked like Thor and can't believe her best friend is a real live Viking. <br><br><i>
  <b> Poppy &amp; Rune, best friends for infinity </b>
</i><br><br>A blossoming, beautiful, friendship that turns into so so much more <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=9hj5gm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457471051i/18364233._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=106c03o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457469477i/18363942.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i> This jar is for you to record your boy-kisses, Poppy. All the kisses that make your heart almost burst, the ones that are the most special, the ones you want to remember when your're old and gray. The ones that will make you smile when you remember them in your mind. </i><br><br>They shared their first ever kiss at the age of 8 <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=iqvvqx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457581781i/18376884.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Count down to One Thousand RUIN Kisses = And my heart almost burst<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=106c03o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457469477i/18363942.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>
  <b> Write down where you were when you were kissed. You'll have a treasure jar of all the precious kisses that made your heart soar.</b>
</i><br><br><b>AGE FIFTEEN </b><br>These two are closer than ever, best friends, kindred spirits, they are never apart, a love so strong even they find it hard to understand. But it is what it is..<br><br>Rune's father has been offered a transfer back to Oslo, it could be weeks, months, years they don't know.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=106c03o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457469477i/18363942.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>
  <b> I'd seen Poppy every day since I was five. Slept beside her almost every night since I was twelve. Kissed her every day since I was eight, and loved her with everything I had so many days I'd stopped keeping track. I had no idea how to live a day without her next to me. How to breathe without her by my side. </b>
</i><br><br>A hasty tear felt, emotional roller coaster of a goodbye <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=106c03o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457469477i/18363942.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>
  <b> “Kiss number three hundred and fifty-four. With my Rune, in the blossom grove … and my heart almost burst. My kisses are all yours, Rune. No one else will ever have these lips but you." </b>
</i><br><br>Promises to keep in touch, talk daily, write to each other.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=106c03o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457469477i/18363942.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>
  <b> Kiss number three hundred and fifty six. With Rune on my drive way when he left.</b>
</i><br> <br>Two long grueling years go by<br><br>Poppy seized all contact, no emails, no phone calls, no texts, she left school, left town, she had vanished, no words, no trace, just gone.<br><br><b> AGED SEVENTEEN </b><br><br>Then words that Poppy never thought she would hear again <i>
  <b>"He's coming back."</b>
</i><br><br>Moving back to where it all started, living next door, his bedroom right opposite hers across the yard. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2i239x" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457581602i/18376874.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i> “Do realize how deeply I feel about you?”<br>I slowly shook my head, needing her to tell me. She placed my hand over her heart and her hand over mine. I felt its steady beat under my palm, the steady beat that got faster as my eyes locked on hers. “It’s like music,” she explained. “When I look at you, when you touch me, when I see your face … when we kiss, my heart plays a song. It sings that it needs you like I need air. It sings to me that I adore you. It sings that I’ve found its perfect missing part.” </i><br><br>It seemed like every page I read had highlighted pieces on them that I wanted to share but then my review would be ridden with more quotes than the actual feels that raced through my body, heart and soul, this book surpassed all my expectations and has become one of my all time favorites from this amazing talented author..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mcu888" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457582188i/18376922._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gods the feels, the train wreck of emotions, my head is thumping, my heart is breaking, my nose is running and my eyes are red and blood shot, I was warned that this book was a tear jerker but I wasn't prepared for how much. This book shattered me, it slayed me, it pulled emotions out that I never knew I had, could feel, this book is just truly beautifully written, this deserves to be read, this book deserves my tears, I will always have a spot in my heart for this book, I loved the depth of love Poppy &amp; Ruin shared, a truly captivating journey..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2i239x" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457582545i/18376960.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>
  <b>Kiss eight hundred and nineteen was the kiss that changed it all. The kiss that proved that a long-haired brooding boy from Norway and a quirky girl from the Deep South could find a love to rival the greats. It showed that love was simply the tenacity to make sure that the other half of your heart knew he, or she, was adored in every way. In every minute of every day. That love was tenderness in its purest form.</b>
</i><br><br>I'm going to leave my review here, go into this with an open heart, an open mind and an open box of tissues..<br><br><i>We were just Poppy &amp; Ruin- there was no beginning to us and no end. </i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2i239x" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457581602i/18376874.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <i> “Rune’s kisses varied. They were slow and soft, gentle and feather-light. Then they were hard, fast and ravishing. Both left me breathless. Both made it into the jar.<br>More kisses sewn onto my heart" </i>
</b><br><br>Even though this book states that it's YA age 14 upwards I think this is suitable for all ages, i don't think at the age of 14 if I would've handled the depth of emotion in this book at that age..<br><br>I'm not afraid to admit that a few times I just had to set my kindle aside and walk away until my emotions had settled..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2zohkkm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457582188i/18376923._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Don't go into this thinking you'll dodge that emotional bullet (like I thought) because it will find you..<br><br><b>MY THOUGHTS</b> <br>Starting these characters from such an early age gives you a glimpse into how their little minds worked, from one handshake it signed their fate as best friends for eternity, even back then you could feel that undeniable bond that these two carried in their hearts. This is so different to any other book I've read by this author, she's definitely upped her game with this book.<br>I've only ever had 2x books that made me fugly cry and they were "Only when it rains' by Lisa De Jong, and "When I fall" by Christine Zolenze, this book brutally kidnapped me and placed me in the twilight zone of emotional overload, it ripped me to shreds, the feels came at me like a roller-coaster of it's tracks, the story line right from the start gripped me in it's hand, had me by the throat until that very last page was read..<br>I laughed, I cried, I loved and yet again I cried and cried and when an author can bring out that strong emotion from an unemotional person deserves more than my 5 stars..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=mwr0r9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457582188i/18376924.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1583065471" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15480265532892124794"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421464i/837220._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥ ♥ ♥ 3.75 STARS ♥ ♥ ♥</b><br/><br/><br/>I have tried writing a review for this book for the past two days and I just can't. So I will show you through gifs how this book made me feel.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When the book started, it seemed like everything was going to be great. Rune and Poppy meet as little kids and I know I'm gonna love them together. But then Poppy's grandma comes into the picture with her thousand boy kisses jar for Poppy and I was all...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458754993ra/18527323.gif' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Then is got so good and so heart warming seeing Poppy and Rune grow up together.</span>
  <span id="freeText15480265532892124794" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421464i/837220._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥ ♥ ♥ 3.75 STARS ♥ ♥ ♥</b><br><br><br>I have tried writing a review for this book for the past two days and I just can't. So I will show you through gifs how this book made me feel.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When the book started, it seemed like everything was going to be great. Rune and Poppy meet as little kids and I know I'm gonna love them together. But then Poppy's grandma comes into the picture with her thousand boy kisses jar for Poppy and I was all...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458754993ra/18527323.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then is got so good and so heart warming seeing Poppy and Rune grow up together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457549005ra/18373489.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I thought everything between Poppy and Rune would stay happy, but in came the sadness...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458755264ra/18527402.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I couldn't wait for the sadness to end. And it seemed like it finally would that I got all happy and excited!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429914582ra/14643118.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unfortunately that didn't last too long. Oh, boy did Tillie Cole butcher me. I couldn't have been more devastated by the turn Poppy and Rune's love story took. My heart just shattered.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458755521ra/18527417.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then that ending...The Leo gif says it all.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458755735ra/18527436.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, that epilogue tho...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445493033ra/16661125.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The best thing I can say to describe this book was that this was an experience, and it freaking destroyed me. It was all hearts and flowers with angst, and so much pain. It was so incredibly bittersweet. If you haven't gotten it from the gifs, you're gonna need a shit ton of tissues at hand when reading this book. I am left emotionally drained that I can barely put words together, hence this short choppy review lol. I really enjoyed their story. The only bad thing I can say is that it was a little too saccharine at times for my taste.<br><br>Rune...was the absolute best! What a hero, he was just perfect for Poppy. And Poppy...I admire her strength and selflessness. This was a really good book, one I won't be forgetting any time soon. If you're looking for a good crying book, this one will have you ugly bawling in no time. <br><br>Okay, well this is as good as this review is gonna get, I'm off to find the fluffiest damn book I can find.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1336555498" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1336555498?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1336555498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8479799894287356407"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457438826i/18359017._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> It's LIVE early!! <br/><a href='http://amzn.to/1XprTgF' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a><br/><a href='http://amzn.to/22eX95B' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a></b><br/><br/><b>10</b><b>
  <i> ‘and our hearts are bursting’</i>
</b><b>stars</b><br/><br/><b>‘Rune pressed a kiss just below my ear and whispered, </b><b>
  <i>“Sleep, baby. I got you.”</i>
</b> <b>And he did. He had me. Just like I had him.’</b><br/><br/>Yet another genre and yet another winner from the supremely talented and versatile Tillie Cole. Not just a winner, but now our favourite of all her books and that’s no easy feat considering we have loved everything this author has written. From the funny to the gritty, from the emotional to th</span>
  <span id="freeText8479799894287356407" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457438826i/18359017._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> It's LIVE early!! <br><a href="http://amzn.to/1XprTgF" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a><br><a href="http://amzn.to/22eX95B" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a></b><br><br><b>10</b><b>
  <i> ‘and our hearts are bursting’</i>
</b><b>stars</b><br><br><b>‘Rune pressed a kiss just below my ear and whispered, </b><b>
  <i>“Sleep, baby. I got you.”</i>
</b> <b>And he did. He had me. Just like I had him.’</b><br><br>Yet another genre and yet another winner from the supremely talented and versatile Tillie Cole. Not just a winner, but now our favourite of all her books and that’s no easy feat considering we have loved everything this author has written. From the funny to the gritty, from the emotional to the uncomfortable, we’re convinced there is <b>NOTHING </b>this lady can’t write and both agree when we say this is <b>THE most beautiful, emotional and stunningly written love story we’ve ever read.</b> This book is as special as special can be.<br><br><b>‘Kiss eight hundred and nineteen was the kiss that changed it all. The kiss that proved that a long-haired brooding boy from Norway and a quirky girl from the Deep South could find a love to rival the greats. It showed that love was simply the tenacity to make sure that the other half of your heart knew he, or she, was adored in every way. In every minute of every day. That love was tenderness in its purest form.’</b><br><br>We’ve enjoyed books, we’ve been moved by books and we’ve cried over books but never and we mean<b> NEVER </b>have we been left so emotionally wrought yet so completely satisfied after finishing a story. We found ourselves talking, sobbing and reliving every exquisite moment, of which there were numerous. And so it was with swollen eyes and overflowing hearts that we chatted into the early hours of the morning never wanting to relinquish our feelings for Poppy and Rune.<br><br><b>‘She knew she had me, just as much as I had her. We were all we needed.’</b><br><br>There wasn’t a page that wasn’t highlighted as this book penetrated our souls and left us feeling so unbelievably thankful and privileged to have experienced this unforgettable story of love in its most beautiful, searing and epic form. A book such as A Thousand Boy Kisses doesn’t come along often, so when it does, we possessively hold each word in our hearts and treasure every single emotion as we did with Rune and Poppy’s story. This story encompasses everything that makes us passionate about reading.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I used to know a boy, a boy I loved with my whole heart, who lived for a single moment. Who told me that a single moment could change the world. It could change someone’s life. That one moment could make someone’s life, in that brief second, infinitely better or infinitely worse”</i>
</b><br><br>Poppy Litchfield and Rune Kristiansen created a bond of friendship at five years old that would blossom into a love story to rival the greats. They truly were two parts of one heart in every sense of the word. Despite their tender years, their love was extraordinary and it was epic and there is no doubt this came across in Tillie’s story as we lived and breathed the enormity of their feelings.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m half a heart. This, who I am now, was due to a life devoid of you. This darkness, this anger, was born from you not being by my side. Poppymin. My adventurer. My girl.”</i>
</b><br><br>Tillie Cole doesn’t have to force emotions from us, they are elicited spontaneously from the natural fluidity of her writing. This lady writes from the heart and not only were our tears falling freely on the pages, but we also felt hers in every word as she brought us the sweetest girl; an old soul with a perception of life that belied her years, and the brooding boy who moved into her street and into her heart. She taught him what it was to love and feel and together they created something that went beyond mere love. Breathtaking doesn’t begin to describe their story. Heartbreaking is an understatement. Uplifting doesn’t do it justice. <b>There really are no words to do this story justice.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>'Maybe we’re like the cherry blossom, Rune. Maybe we loved too much too young and burned so bright that we had to fade out.’</i>
</b><br><br>From the innocence and exuberance of childhood to the confusion and pain of youth, we lived it all. We fought their battles and lived through joy and heartbreak with them yet we haven’t even scratched the surface of their story, you couldn’t imagine for one minute how this story plays out. We know we didn’t.<br><br><b>‘I was going to do this for her. I was going to do my damnedest to make her happy. I’d win her back. I’d win her back as the Rune I was now. There was no choice. This was us. This was our new adventure. ‘</b><br><br> Told in dual POV for optimum effect, there is so much to experience in A Thousand Boy Kisses and we cannot stress enough that you must go into this story<b> spoiler free</b> and experience it all as the author intended. <b>Don’t ask, just feel.</b><br><br>We do love YA stories however we know some readers evade this genre. To those readers we would urge you to still pick this book up. The nature of the story and the delivery from this author is well worth putting those thoughts aside to experience something so positively beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Come say hi and follow us at:<br>✦ <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b><br></span>

<div id="review_1588309691" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1588309691" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30035966-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523817330p2/30035966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1588309691?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781530496198" href="/book/show/29559363-a-thousand-boy-kisses">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1588309691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15236399718401380724">When Rune’s family moves from Norway to Georgia, Rune never expected to love his time there. When he meets the quirky, talented, and shy girl that lives next-door things start to look up for him. Poppy knew the second she met Rune they were going to be best friends and didn’t hold back<br/>letting him know. Over the next few years the two spent every moment together. The two do everything together and as they grow so does their relationship. The two go from best friends to boyfriend and girlfriend.<br/><br/><i>
 </i></span>
  <span id="freeText15236399718401380724" style="display:none">When Rune’s family moves from Norway to Georgia, Rune never expected to love his time there. When he meets the quirky, talented, and shy girl that lives next-door things start to look up for him. Poppy knew the second she met Rune they were going to be best friends and didn’t hold back<br>letting him know. Over the next few years the two spent every moment together. The two do everything together and as they grow so does their relationship. The two go from best friends to boyfriend and girlfriend.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Live hard, love harder. Chase dreams, seek adventures … capture moments. Live beautifully.”</b>
</i><br><br>Sadly, Rune and his family knew that there stay in Georgia wouldn’t be permanent and that they would have to eventually have to return to Norway for a period of time. When his family gets word that they have to return Rune and Poppy decide that even with the distance that they will find a way to work. At first this works out well until one-day Poppy just disappears. Two years later Rune and his family are returning to Georgia and to the house that is still beside Poppy’s the girl he hasn’t spoken to since… Only when Rune returns he isn’t the same sweet boy that Poppy loved. Rune has turned into a bad apple. Smoking, staying out late, and going to parties. <br><br>I heard from every review that this book was a for sure tear-jerker and that the end of the book was going to wreck me… Well here’s what I have to say about that. This book did in fact make me tear up, but it wasn’t the ending, it was the beginning. I did enjoy reading Poppy and Rune’s story once they were older and he returned, but I honestly I preferred reading about their young age more. I loved getting to see these two grow up and how adorable they were as kids. There stolen moments and precious moments really got to me. I loved everything leading up to the night Rune leaves. <br><br><i>
  <b>“because sometimes all we get are moments. There are no do-overs; whatever happens in a moment defines life—perhaps it is life.”</b>
</i><br><br>Once Rune returns, at first, I really enjoyed it. I liked hearing about awkward Poppy and the new bad boy Rune. However, as things progressed and the two start to spend time together again, I found myself getting a little bored. At first things are heated because we are so drawn to know why Poppy all of a sudden vanished. That theme just keeps getting repeated over and over again. The other bad part is that I figured out kind of early on what the big reveal is. It could really only be one of two things… So you’ll probably figure it out too. So with everything being repetitive and the reveal not being that big for me I started to get a little sick of this book. Found myself rushing to the end, not to find out what happened, but to just get the book over with. Rune and Poppy are also pretty generic YA book characters. She even plays the cello… Something we’ve seen several times before… <i>I mean seriously how many people do you know that play the cello?!?!</i> Rune, in my<br>opinion, is the stronger character between the two. He feels more authentic than Poppy. Neither of them really gave me what I was hoping to get out of them. Also the fact that not only did the story repeat, I felt like their relationship in general repeated. By the end of the story I knew where everything was headed right down to events playing out how they did. <br><br><a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9XitTAQfG-U/Vv52myuKZbI/AAAAAAAADbM/JEcBbNE4TtIPI374fTrPJhhgNXq7pHSWA/s1600/sigh.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460819831ra/18792993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><div>
<br><br>I didn’t hate <i>A Thousand Boy Kisses </i> but I didn’t love it either. I think this would be a great<br>intro to YA, but those of you who are a little more seasoned with it might not find it as interesting.<br><br><b>READ THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS OVER ON OUR BLOG: <br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR </a><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR </a><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR</a></b>
</div></span>
  <a data-text-id="15236399718401380724" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1837687414?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/29504138-a-thousand-boy-kisses">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Emotional pain sluts </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=tragic-heartbreaking">tragic-heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1837687414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4866549114089618722"><b>Genre: </b>YA Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone <br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481761970i/21452926.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Poppy Litchfield was only 5 years old when a new boy moved in next door. They became fast friends and had been inseparable since.<br/><br/>Rune Kristiansen had plenty of adventure with Poppy. When they were separated, things completely changed between them. When he finally came back, both of them no longer knew each other. But when the truth that divided them came to the surface, they must decide how to make the love they once</span>
  <span id="freeText4866549114089618722" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>YA Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone <br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481761970i/21452926.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Poppy Litchfield was only 5 years old when a new boy moved in next door. They became fast friends and had been inseparable since.<br><br>Rune Kristiansen had plenty of adventure with Poppy. When they were separated, things completely changed between them. When he finally came back, both of them no longer knew each other. But when the truth that divided them came to the surface, they must decide how to make the love they once had worth all the pain.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had this one under my ugly crying list for a while now but been pushing it back due to the age range. I'm glad I finally read this and enjoyed it regardless of their ages.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“I’ll give you a thousand kisses, Poppymin. All of them. No one will kiss you ever, but me.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Rune. It hurt to see how he evolved from an innocent kid to what he became towards the end of the book. I felt and understood his pain, his fear and his anger.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Being loved by Rune brought the heady sensation of warmth. Being hated by Rune was like standing on an arctic ice shelf.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Poppy was such a cute kid when they first met. Even though socially she was the opposite of Rune, together they just clicked.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“How can a love like ours be broken?"</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>The story was somewhat cute and sweet, but it also hurt. I really like the "thousand boy kisses" element and how it drove the story. It became the source of both smiles and tears.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481761970i/21452927.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A Thousand Boy Kisses is a story of a couple's journey making up for the time they lost. It would appeal to readers looking for emotional reads.<br><br><i> <b>Note: </b><br>If you know me well enough you’d know I don’t do the pink flowers and heart thing on my teasers. But those two elements are significant to the story so there is it lol!</i><br><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451029682i/17500808.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/WarhawkesVault" rel="nofollow noopener">

Until the day Rune has to go back to his home country, Norway, and leave Poppy behind. They promise not to lose contact or forget about each other, but everything changes when Poppy suddenly stops all contact. Two years later, Rune is back on the US and reunited with Poppy once more. But when he finds out why Poppy stopped talking to him he’ll realize the worst is yet to come and som</span>
  <span id="freeText3907793986717893001" style="display:none"><b> 2,5 Heartbreaking Stars. </b>	<br><br>Poppy and Rune grew up together as best friends, until they fall in love as teenagers. Until the day Rune has to go back to his home country, Norway, and leave Poppy behind. They promise not to lose contact or forget about each other, but everything changes when Poppy suddenly stops all contact. Two years later, Rune is back on the US and reunited with Poppy once more. But when he finds out why Poppy stopped talking to him he’ll realize the worst is yet to come and sometimes not even all our wishes are enough. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459250952i/18586527.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*Some spoilers may be ahead*</i><br>After reading TFiOS, A Walk to Remember and some similar stories I promised to myself that I was done with this kind of books. As good as they are, they aren’t worth the heartbreak. And if Tillie Cole wasn’t one of my favorites and “auto-buy” authors, if this cover wasn’t gorgeous and if I hadn’t jump on this book without knowing anything about it, honestly, I would have never read it. <br>Don’t get me wrong, this is a powerful story and it’s brilliantly written (as Tillie Cole got us used to by now), but it’s also full of clichés and with a development and an ending that just left me completely depressed, in the end of the day that is not what I’m looking in a book. <br>Imagine if all your tearjerkers YA books got high on cocaine together and had a son: this book would be that son. <br>If you don’t mind the tears and heartbreak, go ahead: this book is definitely for you. Unfortunately, for me, it was a little too much. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429744792i/14626262.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 2,5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> Poppy was a sweet and strong girl and it was easy to understand her actions. Rune was sweet and caring as well, and a easy to like hero. They both were a little immature at times, but they were 17, so we should be expecting it. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Not really. This is YA after all. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Cancer.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Some may say this is an “unconventional” happy ending.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1557193733?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1557193733" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7138908650872336671"><b>5 A Thousand Stars</b><br/><br/>If you are curious about this book, I highly suggest you read this book blindly. It’s a sweet Young Adult book that will grip and melt your heart. <br/><br/>Not only do I love the cover, the author, but the storyline was very profound and very emotional. If you are looking for a dramatic book with an epic love, A Thousand Boy Kisses is just for you, but that’s no surprise right? Tillie Cole rarely disappoints me.<br/><br/>It’s about two young lovers, childhood lovers since the age of five. It’s ad</span>
  <span id="freeText7138908650872336671" style="display:none"><b>5 A Thousand Stars</b><br><br>If you are curious about this book, I highly suggest you read this book blindly. It’s a sweet Young Adult book that will grip and melt your heart. <br><br>Not only do I love the cover, the author, but the storyline was very profound and very emotional. If you are looking for a dramatic book with an epic love, A Thousand Boy Kisses is just for you, but that’s no surprise right? Tillie Cole rarely disappoints me.<br><br>It’s about two young lovers, childhood lovers since the age of five. It’s adorable and I love the innocent relationship between Rune and Poppy. There’s something so profound about the love they have for each other. It’s the once-in-a-lifetime kind of love that you ache and breathe for. I was addicting to their tale and I couldn’t stop reading. You will have to block off hours of the day because you will read this in one sitting. I promise. <br><br>The book is written from both POV, which I enjoyed a lot because I had to see the story from both sides. There’s so much to this book with heartache, regrets and undeniable love. The thing that makes it so good is all the emotions Tillie makes you feel. You feel like you are taking the journey with the characters and I love it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ll give you a thousand kisses, Poppymin. All of them. No one will kiss you ever, but me”<br><br>“I could see the fierceness of that possession in his stare. I could feel it in his grip on my hand. And I liked it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really can’t say anymore. It’s a journey and real treat Tillie takes you on. I have no regrets and wishing my husband was home so he can give me a thousand kisses. <br><br><i>An ARC was provided</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25912358.A_Thousand_Boy_Kisses" title="A Thousand Boy Kisses by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1453299050s/25912358.jpg" alt="A Thousand Boy Kisses by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
