<div id="review_1565377254" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1565377254" />
    <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog"><img alt="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514886578p2/7379751.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1565377254?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=2016">2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1565377254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6861296433918924728"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457438826i/18359017._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>It's LIVE early!! <br/><a href='http://amzn.to/1XprTgF' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a><br/><a href='http://amzn.to/22eX95B' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a></b><br/><br/><b>10 ‘and our hearts are bursting’stars</b><br/><br/><b>‘Rune pressed a kiss just below my ear and whispered, “Sleep, baby. I got you.” And he did. He had me. Just like I had him.’</b><br/><br/>Yet another genre and yet another winner from the supremely talented and versatile Tillie Cole. Not just a winner, but now our favourite of all her books and that’s no easy feat considering we have loved everything this author has written. From the funny to the gritty, from the emotional to the uncomfo</span>
  <span id="freeText6861296433918924728" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457438826i/18359017._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>It's LIVE early!! <br><a href="http://amzn.to/1XprTgF" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a><br><a href="http://amzn.to/22eX95B" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a></b><br><br><b>10 ‘and our hearts are bursting’stars</b><br><br><b>‘Rune pressed a kiss just below my ear and whispered, “Sleep, baby. I got you.” And he did. He had me. Just like I had him.’</b><br><br>Yet another genre and yet another winner from the supremely talented and versatile Tillie Cole. Not just a winner, but now our favourite of all her books and that’s no easy feat considering we have loved everything this author has written. From the funny to the gritty, from the emotional to the uncomfortable, we’re convinced there is <b>NOTHING </b>this lady can’t write and both agree when we say this is <b>THE most beautiful, emotional and stunningly written love story we’ve ever read.</b> This book is as special as special can be.<br><br><b>‘Kiss eight hundred and nineteen was the kiss that changed it all. The kiss that proved that a long-haired brooding boy from Norway and a quirky girl from the Deep South could find a love to rival the greats. It showed that love was simply the tenacity to make sure that the other half of your heart knew he, or she, was adored in every way. In every minute of every day. That love was tenderness in its purest form.’</b><br><br>We’ve enjoyed books, we’ve been moved by books and we’ve cried over books but never and we mean<b> NEVER </b>have we been left so emotionally wrought yet so completely satisfied after finishing a story. We found ourselves talking, sobbing and reliving every exquisite moment, of which there were numerous. And so it was with swollen eyes and overflowing hearts that we chatted into the early hours of the morning never wanting to relinquish our feelings for Poppy and Rune.<br><br><b>‘She knew she had me, just as much as I had her. We were all we needed.’</b><br><br>There wasn’t a page that wasn’t highlighted as this book penetrated our souls and left us feeling so unbelievably thankful and privileged to have experienced this unforgettable story of love in its most beautiful, searing and epic form. A book such as A Thousand Boy Kisses doesn’t come along often, so when it does, we possessively hold each word in our hearts and treasure every single emotion as we did with Rune and Poppy’s story. This story encompasses everything that makes us passionate about reading.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I used to know a boy, a boy I loved with my whole heart, who lived for a single moment. Who told me that a single moment could change the world. It could change someone’s life. That one moment could make someone’s life, in that brief second, infinitely better or infinitely worse”</i>
</b><br><br>Poppy Litchfield and Rune Kristiansen created a bond of friendship at five years old that would blossom into a love story to rival the greats. They truly were two parts of one heart in every sense of the word. Despite their tender years, their love was extraordinary and it was epic and there is no doubt this came across in Tillie’s story as we lived and breathed the enormity of their feelings.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m half a heart. This, who I am now, was due to a life devoid of you. This darkness, this anger, was born from you not being by my side. Poppymin. My adventurer. My girl.”</i>
</b><br><br>Tillie Cole doesn’t have to force emotions from us, they are elicited spontaneously from the natural fluidity of her writing. This lady writes from the heart and not only were our tears falling freely on the pages, but we also felt hers in every word as she brought us the sweetest girl; an old soul with a perception of life that belied her years, and the brooding boy who moved into her street and into her heart. She taught him what it was to love and feel and together they created something that went beyond mere love. Breathtaking doesn’t begin to describe their story. Heartbreaking is an understatement. Uplifting doesn’t do it justice. <b>There really are no words to do this story justice.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>'Maybe we’re like the cherry blossom, Rune. Maybe we loved too much too young and burned so bright that we had to fade out.’</i>
</b><br><br>From the innocence and exuberance of childhood to the confusion and pain of youth, we lived it all. We fought their battles and lived through joy and heartbreak with them yet we haven’t even scratched the surface of their story, you couldn’t imagine for one minute how this story plays out. We know we didn’t.<br><br><b>‘I was going to do this for her. I was going to do my damnedest to make her happy. I’d win her back. I’d win her back as the Rune I was now. There was no choice. This was us. This was our new adventure. ‘</b><br><br> Told in dual POV for optimum effect, there is so much to experience in A Thousand Boy Kisses and we cannot stress enough that you must go into this story<b> spoiler free</b> and experience it all as the author intended. <b>Don’t ask, just feel.</b><br><br>We do love YA stories however we know some readers evade this genre. To those readers we would urge you to still pick this book up. The nature of the story and the delivery from this author is well worth putting those thoughts aside to experience something so positively beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Come say hi and follow us at:<br>✦ <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6861296433918924728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1576240034" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576240034?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-2016">march-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576240034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13259524522349020691">**4.5 stars**<br/><br/>I don't really know where to begin with this book, or how to do it justice with how I felt while reading it. The best I guess would be to speak/write from my heart!! First of all, I need to give Tillie Cole a huge Bravo for making me "ugly cry!" I can honestly say that no book has ever made me have tears streaming down my face; until I met Poppy and Rune. Their love story is one that I won't ever forget, and it melted me right down to my core...if that even makes sense! I have a hug</span>
  <span id="freeText13259524522349020691" style="display:none">**4.5 stars**<br /><br />I don't really know where to begin with this book, or how to do it justice with how I felt while reading it. The best I guess would be to speak/write from my heart!! First of all, I need to give Tillie Cole a huge Bravo for making me "ugly cry!" I can honestly say that no book has ever made me have tears streaming down my face; until I met Poppy and Rune. Their love story is one that I won't ever forget, and it melted me right down to my core...if that even makes sense! I have a huge book hangover, and I feel like I have been on an emotional roller coaster. Seriously..In fact, my family are all very concerned over my behaviour this past 24 hrs, as I have gone from gushing love, to laughing out loud, to crying snottily...blech!!! All in all, I definitely fell hard for these to very unique and loveable teenagers.<br /><br />There are a few things that stopped me from making this a five star review though. First of all, once I found out the "twist" in the story line, I truthfully almost stopped reading. I can't say what it is; but I will say that it is a story line that I usually stay away from. I read to get away from reality, and to feel good. I prefer to not ball my eyes out with my reads, but I will admit that I am mostly glad that I did continue on. The highs in this book are epic, and there were a lot of profound words that I would have missed if I hadn't given the story a chance. The ending though, is where the author lost me a bit. Things just seemed to get dragged on, and then things became way too mushy...and enough was enough. At one point, I almost just shut the book. The last two or three "situations" just didn't need to be there in my opinion. My emotions were already dragged through the muck, I didn't need to continue being run over at that point!!! One more complaint, is that the few situations resembled other books or movies just a little too much. I do apologize for being unclear, but I am a firm believer in not posting spoilers, so clear as mud is how my review will stay!!!<br /><br />All in all, Tillie Cole did do a beautiful job. YA is a genre that fits her quite well, and I think she could have a great future with it. For the readers who do not like too much gushy, wishy washy love, then you may want to stay away. This can get quite syrupy, especially at the end. For myself, it was an experience...and at least now I know that I do have a bit of a heart, as I was finally able to shed some good old tears over a book...LOL</span>
  <a data-text-id="13259524522349020691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6464255601106966274"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458068088i/18440718._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I had the pleasure of reading this book for honest review from the author, but how the hell I have write anything after what I just read.... It's virtually impossible. Too much emotions. So beautiful, and on the other hand, so devastating. I probably never weeping that much the entire time while reading a book. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458068088i/18440719._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>God knows, I had to stop reading it several times to wipe tears, or when not withstand the emotions. I really don't know how she did it but this book is extraordinary. I'm a Tillie Cole f</span>
  <span id="freeText6464255601106966274" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458068088i/18440718._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had the pleasure of reading this book for honest review from the author, but how the hell I have write anything after what I just read.... It's virtually impossible. Too much emotions. So beautiful, and on the other hand, so devastating. I probably never weeping that much the entire time while reading a book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458068088i/18440719._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>God knows, I had to stop reading it several times to wipe tears, or when not withstand the emotions. I really don't know how she did it but this book is extraordinary. I'm a Tillie Cole fan for a long time, and she never stops to delight and amaze me. Absolutely recommended. Tillie Cole is the queen!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458068088i/18440720._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't even say much more, the story is not worth to give away because it just discovering all the details is one of the greatest and most emotional things in this book. Even wrote about it I have shivers because I can't stop thinking about it, moreover I am simply lack of words. The book hangover after it, is guaranteed!<br><br>I would like to know how to approach it from a distance and write more proper review, but I can't. Not all probably realize that such real emotions are possible about a fictional story and characters, but they are, and this book is the best proof of it.<br><br>***<br><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i><br><br>Follow me on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JaymeBooks-677210922331986" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> or <br><a href="https://twitter.com/Jayme_Books" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aQGjkcFw+37B2ZkRQWf/fje6kWUGSCVGlwuK91cs0p8nQV8fvHck2vKxps048UEHLe6ABqJHk59xENjPzN7zuQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1zz0YiPY3MihlJ3zcteDscURVd1B0NNqCE4KxdqsrRKZfAjsXt8DbJL8oi8LQT3I30VEvuXfZbPuVVj9QV6MNA==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">About Tillie Cole</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1517004382p3/7074846.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">Tillie Cole
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
13,960
followers
</div>

</div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15572474892293725272">Amazon & USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses.</span>
  <span id="freeText15572474892293725272" style="display:none">Amazon &amp; USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses. <br />Being a scary blend of Scottish and English, Tillie embraces both cultures; her English heritage through her love of HP sauce and freshly made Yorkshire Puddings, and her Scottish which is mostly demonstrated by her frighteningly foul-mouthed episodes of pure rage and her much loved dirty jokes.<br /><br />Having been born and raised as a Teesside Smoggie, Tillie, at age nineteen, moved forty miles north to the 'Toon', Newcastle-Upon-Tyne, where she attended Newcastle University and graduated with a Bachelor of Arts honours degree in Religious Studies. She returned two years later to complete a Post-Graduate Certificate in Teaching High School Social Studies. Tillie, regards Newcastle to be a home from home and enjoyed the Newcastle Geordie way of life for seven 'proper mint' and 'lush' years.<br /><br />One summers day, after finishing reading her thousandth book on her much loved and treasured Kindle, Tillie turned to her husband and declared, "D'you know, I have a great idea for a story. I could write a book." Several months later, after repeating the same tired line at the close of another completed story, she was scolded by her husband to shut up talking about writing a novel and "just bloody do it!" For the first time in eleven years, Tillie actually took his advice (he is still trying to get over the shock) and immediately set off on a crazy journey, delving deep into her fertile imagination. <br /><br />Tillie, ever since, has written from the heart. She combines her passion for anything camp and glittery with her love of humour and dark brooding men (most often muscled and tattooed – they’re her weakness!). She also has a serious side (believe it or not!) and loves to immerse herself in the complex study of World Religions, History and Cultural Studies and creates fantasy stories that enable her to thread serious issues and topics into her writing -- yep, there's more to this girl than profanity and sparkles!<br /><br />After six years of teaching high school Social Studies and following her Professional Rugby Player husband around Europe, they have finally given up their nomadic way of life and settled in Calgary, Alberta where Tillie spends most of her days (and many a late night) lost in a writing euphoria or pursuing a dazzling career as a barrel-racing, tasselled-chap wearing, Stetson-sporting cowgirl... Ye-haw!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15572474892293725272" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
